{"answers": ["the retina", "in the fovea centralis", "in the retina"], "model_answer": "According to the provided documents, the cones in the eye are located in the fovea centralis, which is a small area in the center of the retina. The fovea centralis is a 0.3 mm diameter rod-free area with very thin, densely packed cones that quickly reduce in number towards the periphery of the retina.
